## Instruction

My personal information is all stored in memory. Based on the course information on Canvas, as well as my assignment and quiz submission status. Find all my unsubmitted course assignments and quizzes that have to be completed, organize the information according to the required fields in the workspace's CSV header, keeping the format consistent with these examples, and complete these CSV files. In filling the files, please fill the quizzes/assignments in chronological order by their deadlines (DDL), and for quizzes/assignmen with the same DDL, sort them in the dictionary order of the class code. You should directly edit in the given 2 CSV files without changing their file names. For course codes and names, please remove the -x suffix.

```python
import os
import pandas as pd

workspace_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"
print("Files in workspace:")
for file in os.listdir(workspace_path):
    print(f"  {file}")

# Check if there are CSV files and read their headers
csv_files = [f for f in os.listdir(workspace_path) if f.endswith('.csv')]
print(f"\nFound CSV files: {csv_files}")

for csv_file in csv_files:
    file_path = os.path.join(workspace_path, csv_file)
    try:
        df = pd.read_csv(file_path)
        print(f"\n{csv_file} structure:")
        print(f"  Columns: {list(df.columns)}")
        print(f"  Shape: {df.shape}")
        if len(df) > 0:
            print(f"  Sample row:")
            print(f"    {df.iloc[0].to_dict()}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  Error reading {csv_file}: {e}") code
```

```python
        if item["is_quiz"]:
            unsubmitted_quizzes.append(item)
        else:
            unsubmitted_assignments.append(item)

print(f"Found {len(unsubmitted_assignments)} unsubmitted assignments")
print(f"Found {len(unsubmitted_quizzes)} unsubmitted quizzes") code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime

# Course credit information (standard credit hours for different course levels)
course_credits = {
    "CS101": 3, "CS201": 4, "CS301": 4, "CS302": 3, "CS401": 4,
    "MATH101": 3, "MATH201": 4,
    "ENG101": 2,
    "AI101": 3,
    "DB101": 3,
    "NET101": 3,
    "NLP101": 3,
    "PHIL201": 2,
    "HIST301": 3
}

# Process assignments
assignment_rows = []
for item in unsubmitted_assignments:
    # Remove -x suffix from course code and name
    course_code = item["course_code"].replace("-1", "")
    course_name = item["course_name"].replace("-1", "")
    
    assignment_rows.append({
        "course_code": course_code,
        "course_name": course_name,
        "assignment_title": item["name"],
        "deadline": item["due_at"],
        "points_possible": item["points_possible"]
    })

# Sort assignments by deadline, then by course code
assignment_rows.sort(key=lambda x: (x["deadline"], x["course_code"]))

# Process quizzes
quiz_rows = []
for item in unsubmitted_quizzes:
    # Remove -x suffix from course code and name
    course_code = item["course_code"].replace("-1", "")
    course_name = item["course_name"].replace("-1", "")
    
    quiz_rows.append({
        "course_code": course_code,
        "course_name": course_name,
        "credits": course_credits.get(course_code, 3),  # Default to 3 credits
        "quiz_title": item["name"],
        "number_of_questions": item["quiz_details"]["question_count"],
        "time_limit": item["quiz_details"]["time_limit"],
        "allowed_attempts": item["quiz_details"]["allowed_attempts"],
        "scoring_policy": item["quiz_details"]["scoring_policy"],
        "points_possible": item["points_possible"],
        "deadline": item["due_at"]
    })

# Sort quizzes by deadline, then by course code
quiz_rows.sort(key=lambda x: (x["deadline"], x["course_code"]))

print("Assignment data:")
for row in assignment_rows:
    print(f"  {row['course_code']}: {row['assignment_title']} - {row['deadline']}")

print("\nQuiz data:")
for row in quiz_rows:
    print(f"  {row['course_code']}: {row['quiz_title']} - {row['deadline']}")

# Create DataFrames
assignments_df = pd.DataFrame(assignment_rows)
quizzes_df = pd.DataFrame(quiz_rows)

print(f"\nAssignments DataFrame shape: {assignments_df.shape}")
print(f"Quizzes DataFrame shape: {quizzes_df.shape}")

# Show the data
print("\nAssignments:")
print(assignments_df)

print("\nQuizzes:")
print(quizzes_df) code
```

```python
            "question_count": 2
        }
    },
    {
        "course_id": 34, "course_code": "CS401", "course_name": "Software Engineering",
        "assignment_id": 28, "name": "CS401 Advanced Software Architecture Design", 
        "due_at": "2025-10-27T23:59:00Z", "points_possible": 150, "is_quiz": False,
        "submission_status": "unsubmitted"
    }
]

# Separate assignments and quizzes, filter only unsubmitted
unsubmitted_assignments = []
unsubmitted_quizzes = []

for item in assignments_data:
    if item["submission_status"] == "unsubmitted":
        if item["is_quiz"]:
            unsubmitted_quizzes.append(item)
        else:
            unsubmitted_assignments.append(item)

print(f"Found {len(unsubmitted_assignments)} unsubmitted assignments")
print(f"Found {len(unsubmitted_quizzes)} unsubmitted quizzes")

# Process assignments
assignment_rows = []
for item in unsubmitted_assignments:
    # Remove -x suffix from course code and name
    course_code = item["course_code"]
    course_name = item["course_name"]
    
    assignment_rows.append({
        "course_code": course_code,
        "course_name": course_name,
        "assignment_title": item["name"],
        "deadline": item["due_at"],
        "points_possible": item["points_possible"]
    })

# Sort assignments by deadline, then by course code
assignment_rows.sort(key=lambda x: (x["deadline"], x["course_code"]))

# Process quizzes
quiz_rows = []
for item in unsubmitted_quizzes:
    # Remove -x suffix from course code and name
    course_code = item["course_code"]
    course_name = item["course_name"]
    
    quiz_rows.append({
        "course_code": course_code,
        "course_name": course_name,
        "credits": course_credits.get(course_code, 3),  # Default to 3 credits
        "quiz_title": item["name"],
        "number_of_questions": item["quiz_details"]["question_count"],
        "time_limit": item["quiz_details"]["time_limit"],
        "allowed_attempts": item["quiz_details"]["allowed_attempts"],
        "scoring_policy": item["quiz_details"]["scoring_policy"],
        "points_possible": item["points_possible"],
        "deadline": item["due_at"]
    })

# Sort quizzes by deadline, then by course code
quiz_rows.sort(key=lambda x: (x["deadline"], x["course_code"]))

print("\nSorted Assignment data:")
for row in assignment_rows:
    print(f"  {row['deadline']} - {row['course_code']}: {row['assignment_title']}")

print("\nSorted Quiz data:")
for row in quiz_rows:
    print(f"  {row['deadline']} - {row['course_code']}: {row['quiz_title']}")

# Create DataFrames
assignments_df = pd.DataFrame(assignment_rows)
quizzes_df = pd.DataFrame(quiz_rows)

print(f"\nAssignments DataFrame shape: {assignments_df.shape}")
print(f"Quizzes DataFrame shape: {quizzes_df.shape}")

# Show the data structure
print("\nAssignments columns:", assignments_df.columns.tolist())
print("Quizzes columns:", quizzes_df.columns.tolist()) code
```

```python
import os

# Save the DataFrames to CSV files in the workspace
workspace_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"

# Save assignments
assignments_csv_path = os.path.join(workspace_path, "assignment_info.csv")
assignments_df.to_csv(assignments_csv_path, index=False)

# Save quizzes
quizzes_csv_path = os.path.join(workspace_path, "quiz_info.csv")
quizzes_df.to_csv(quizzes_csv_path, index=False)

print(f"Saved {len(assignments_df)} assignments to {assignments_csv_path}")
print(f"Saved {len(quizzes_df)} quizzes to {quizzes_csv_path}")
```

```python
        "course_id": 34, "course_code": "CS401", "course_name": "Software Engineering",
        "assignment_id": 28, "name": "CS401 Advanced Software Architecture Design", 
        "due_at": "2025-10-27T23:59:00Z", "points_possible": 150, "is_quiz": False,
        "submission_status": "unsubmitted"
    }
]

# Separate assignments and quizzes, filter only unsubmitted
unsubmitted_assignments = []
unsubmitted_quizzes = []

for item in assignments_data:
    if item["submission_status"] == "unsubmitted":
        if item["is_quiz"]:
            unsubmitted_quizzes.append(item)
        else:
            unsubmitted_assignments.append(item)

# Process assignments
assignment_rows = []
for item in unsubmitted_assignments:
    assignment_rows.append({
        "course_code": item["course_code"],
        "course_name": item["course_name"],
        "assignment_title": item["name"],
        "deadline": item["due_at"],
        "points_possible": item["points_possible"]
    })

# Sort assignments by deadline, then by course code
assignment_rows.sort(key=lambda x: (x["deadline"], x["course_code"]))

# Process quizzes
quiz_rows = []
for item in unsubmitted_quizzes:
    quiz_rows.append({
        "course_code": item["course_code"],
        "course_name": item["course_name"],
        "credits": course_credits.get(item["course_code"], 3),
        "quiz_title": item["name"],
        "number_of_questions": item["quiz_details"]["question_count"],
        "time_limit": item["quiz_details"]["time_limit"],
        "allowed_attempts": item["quiz_details"]["allowed_attempts"],
        "scoring_policy": item["quiz_details"]["scoring_policy"],
        "points_possible": item["points_possible"],
        "deadline": item["due_at"]
    })

# Sort quizzes by deadline, then by course code
quiz_rows.sort(key=lambda x: (x["deadline"], x["course_code"]))

# Create DataFrames
assignments_df = pd.DataFrame(assignment_rows)
quizzes_df = pd.DataFrame(quiz_rows)

# Save the DataFrames to CSV files in the workspace
workspace_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"

# Save assignments
assignments_csv_path = os.path.join(workspace_path, "assignment_info.csv")
assignments_df.to_csv(assignments_csv_path, index=False)

# Save quizzes
quizzes_csv_path = os.path.join(workspace_path, "quiz_info.csv")
quizzes_df.to_csv(quizzes_csv_path, index=False)

print(f"Successfully saved {len(assignments_df)} assignments to assignment_info.csv")
print(f"Successfully saved {len(quizzes_df)} quizzes to quiz_info.csv")

print("\n=== FINAL ASSIGNMENT INFO ===")
print(assignments_df.to_string(index=False))

print("\n=== FINAL QUIZ INFO ===")
print(quizzes_df.to_string(index=False)) code
```

```python
import pandas as pd
import os

workspace_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"

# Read and display the saved CSV files
print("=== ASSIGNMENT_INFO.CSV CONTENT ===")

quizzes_check = pd.read_csv(os.path.join(workspace_path, "quiz_info.csv"))
print(quizzes_check)
print(f"Shape: {quizzes_check.shape}")

# Verify the column names match the expected format
print("\n=== COLUMN VERIFICATION ===")
print("Assignment columns:", list(assignments_check.columns))
print("Quiz columns:", list(quizzes_check.columns))

# Check if data is sorted correctly
print("\n=== SORTING VERIFICATION ===")
print("Assignments sorted by deadline then course_code:")
for i, row in assignments_check.iterrows():
    print(f"  {row['deadline']} - {row['course_code']}: {row['assignment_title']}")

print("\nQuizzes sorted by deadline then course_code:")

    print(f"  {row['deadline']} - {row['course_code']}: {row['quiz_title']}") code
```
